 is din bacchon ke adhikaar, dekhbhaal or shiksha ke bare main logon ko jaagruk kiya jaataa he

 Pandit Nehru worked a lot for the education, progress and welfare of children after India's independence
 20 november ko hota tha bal divasasaal 1925 se bal diwas manaaya jane laga or 1953 main duniya bhar main ise manyata mili
 The United Nations announced the celebration of November 20 as Children's Day, but it is celebrated on different days in other countries
 bharat main bhi pehle yah 20 november ko hi manaaya jaataa tha, lekin 1964 main pradhanmantri jawaharlal nehru ke nidhan ke baad sarvasahmati se ye faisla liya gaya ki jawaharlal nehru ke janmdin ko bal diwas ke taur par mana jaae
 In this way, India got a Children's Day apart from the world
 aaj bhi sabake dilon main jinda hai pandit jawaharlal nehru
 
 
 The International Children's Day aims to promote good upbringing of children around the world
 bharat main 14 november ko khaas taur par skulon main tarah-tarah kii mjedaar gatividhiyaan, fansy dress compatishan or melon kaa aayojan hota he

 aapkaa anujakapil mishra There is an age-old tradition of party-changing Indian politics in the election season
 loksabhaa ho yaa vidhansabha chunaav, suvidhanusaar netaaon kaa paala badalanaa aam baat najar aati he
 It was also seen in the recent Maharashtra and Haryana Assembly elections
 khaskar, maharashtra main vipakshi congress or ensipi ke netaa bad sankhya main bijepi or shivasena ke paale main aae
 However, when the results were out, bringing such leaders to the BJP was also seen as overwhelming
 maharashtra main bijepi-shivasena gathbandhan ko 288 main 200 se zyada siton par jeet kii ummid thi
 But when the results came, both the parties were reduced to 161 seats
 yahaan tak ki pankaja munde samet kai mantri bhi chunaav haar gaye
 Shivaji's descendant Udayanraje Bhosale left the NCP in September to join the BJP
 bijepi ke tikat bhosle ne chunaav bhi ladaa or 1 lakh se zyada maton se haar kaa munh dekhnaa padaa
 In the by-elections, the effect was not only in the assembly elections, but also in the by-elections, such leaders of BJP had to face defeat, who came in its court just before the election
 gujarat vidhansabha upachunaav main radhanpur seat se alpesh thakor ne chunaav ladaa or unhen shikast jhelni padi
 Thakor left the Congress and joined BJP in July
 sirf duusare dalon se aae netaa hi bijepi par baari nahin pade, balki nae chehron ko mauka dena bhi uske paksh main nahin gaya he
 In Falehariana assembly elections, the BJP gave a chance to many new and star faces, but they could not do wonders
 pahalwaan babita phogot or yogeshwar dutt ko bijepi ne maidan main utaara, lekin donon baaji haar gaye
 In Maharashtra and Haryana, a factor of not getting the expected results is also considered to be giving entry to external leaders
 bijepi kaaryakartaaon main yah bhaavana he ki party or sanghathan ke vafaadaaron ko kinare kar bahari logon ko chunaav main utaarne kii keemat chukaani padati he
 In Maharashtra too, it has been seen in many places, where the old leaders of BJP were given tickets from other parties and those BJP leaders won the election by contesting as independents
 aise baagi ummidavaar bhi bijepi ke graph main giravat kii badi vajah bane
 The tradition continues in Jharkhand, after the Maharashtra and Haryana assembly elections, in Jharkhand too

 iske alaava rashtriya swasthya beemaa yojana pehle se chal rahi he
 There is an insurance of Rs 50,000 for illness or surgery, whose premium has to be paid from Rs 700 to 800 for a year
 paanch lakh beemaa kaa premium kitna hoga, koun degaa
 When asked by Revenue Secretary Hansmukh Adhia, Vikram Chandra said that when there is a large scale of insurance, the premium will be reduced
 aadhia ne kaha ki iskaa 60 fisadi hissaa centre degaa or 40 fisadi hissaa rajya denge
 October will come to decide what the model of this plan will be, and to launch everything
 unhone yah bhi kaha ki ho saktaa he ki is puure saal ke liye yah beemaa uplabdh na ho magar sarkaar iske liye patibaddh he
 This question also came up in press talks with the Finance Minister
 tippaniyan The answer to the premium question is not available yet
 aapane dekha ki pachaas hazaar ke swasthya beemaa ke liye 700-800 kaa premium lagata he
 If Apollo gets five lakh cashless insurance for the family of four people of Munich, then the premium becomes Rs 17,391 after adding 18 percent GST
 neshnal insurance kaa premium hoga 13,000 rupee tak
 This is an approximate amount
 sarkaar jab niti banaaegi tabhi saaf hoga ki iskaa bajet kya hoga
 The total health budget is only 52000 crores, which is not enough
 down tu arth ke kundan pandey ne is par ek lekh likhaa he, bajet ke turant baad
 Kundan says whether this is a new plan
 2015-16 ke bajet main vitt mantri ne isi tarah kaha tha ki ek lakh kaa beemaa pariwaron ko milegaa
 The Prime Minister also included in his speech on 15 August 2016
 abhi tak yah prastaav november 2016 se cabinet ke paas padaa he
 Private hospitals have warmly welcomed this decision
 zaahir he unki kamai hogi
 a hospital has also been announced for every three parliamentary constituencies
 dedh lakh swasthya aarogy centre banane kii baat hui he
 Will this be the model of Mohalla Clinic, will have to see
 iske alaava vitt mantri ne kaha he ki 4, 46 ganga graamon ko, jo nadi ke kinare based hai, khule main shouch se mukt kiya ja chukaa he, to aap ise khud bhi check kar sakate hai
 There is no cut in income tax, but this does not mean that there is nothing in this budget
 bahut kuch he padhane ke liye
 If 76 percent of the women are getting Mudra loan then what is the effect on the land
 reporting to band ho chuki he, pataa nahin
 It may not be that the big change is lost from the eyes or that we can blindly believe the figures claiming the name of the change
 sarkari naukari ke rojgaar ko lekar kuch bhi nahin kaha gaya, magar ye zarur kaha gaya ki group si or di main intervyuu khatm kar dene se samay bachaa he
 i wish i could be told that how much time is left by removing the interview, which is taking two to three years to complete each recruitment process
 kharif kii fasal kaa time abhi nahin aayaa he
 The time for the Rabi harvest is coming
 march-april main gehun katane lagegaa tab pataa chalegaa ki sarkaar laagat kaa dedh guna detii he yaa nahin
 There is currently no public information
 kya kisaanon ko prati quintal gehun kaa daam 3517 rupee milegaa? ham bas itnaa bataa rahe hai ki sarkaar ne abhi tak dedh guna kabhi nahin diya he
 1625 per quintal is fixed for 2017-18
 dekhte hai 3750 rupee prati quintal kaa bhav miltaa he yaa nahin, kuch hi dinon kii baat he
 At present only six percent farmers get the benefit of MSP
 vitt mantri ne kaha he sabhi ko mili isliye niti ayog centre or rajya sarkaron ke bich charchaa hogi
 But Minister Narendra Tomar has said that the system of awarding MSP is not right
 aalu-pyaaz or tomamter ke kisaanon ko nuksaan se bachaane ke liye 500 karod oparation greens naam kii yojana banaai gai he jo in fasalon ke kisaanon ko vyavsaayik prabandhan apnaane ke liye protsaahit karegi
 When the Yogi government came to Uttar Pradesh last year, it was announced that the government would buy one lakh metric tonnes of potatoes from potato farmers at the rate of Rs 487 per quintal
 yah kuch bhi nahin he
 Last year itself, 160 lakh metric tons of potato was produced in UP
 160 lakh metric ton kaa ek lakh metric ton kharidne kaa elaan kuch bhi nahin tha magar phir bhi kisaanon ko ummid hui ki kuch to milegaa
 By December, potato farmers started throwing their potatoes on the streets
 aalu kisaanon kaa kahana tha ki laagat se bahut kam daam mil rahaa he
 They do not have the benefit of a penny, while the cost of cold storage comes from 900 to 1000 per quintal
 media kii khabaron se pataa chalata he ki upi sarkaar ne ek lakh ton aalu kharidne kaa vaada kiya tha, magar kahin bhi kharide jane kaa aankada nahin mila
 According to a report by Quint, 1300 quintal potatoes were purchased
 agra zile ke aalu kisaan vikaas samiti ke adhyaksh rajvir lavaania to kehete hai ki agra se nau quintal kharida gaya
 Millions of tonnes of potatoes are produced in UP, its one lakh metric tons is nothing
 ham apni taraf se in aankadon kii pushti nahin kar rahe hai lekin rajvir ne kaha upi sarkaar ne up mukhyamantri keshav prasad maury kii adhyakshata main ek samiti banaai he jo aalu kaa bhav nirdhaarit karegi
 Potato farmers are asking for a price of 1000 to 1500 rupees per quintal
 kisaanon ko upaj kaa daam kitna milegaa, yah aane vaale dinon main saaf hoga, philhal aisa koi aankada nahin he jisase pataa chalata ho ki rabi kii upaj kii keemat laagat se dedh guna dene kaa faisla kiya gaya he
 11 lakh crores will be available for loans to farmers this year
 sarkaar ne ek bada faisla yah liya he ki bantai kisaanon ke liye bhi lone uplabdh ho
 For this, NITI Aayog will create a mechanism after talking to the state governments
 tantra kya hoga, kab tak banegaa iskaa ullekh nahin he

 ek anumaanit raashi he ye
